  MOAOA:      tasks distributed to EDGE/FOG/CLOUD by optimizer
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  Metric                           Cloud-Only         MOAOA              Improvement    
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  Total Tasks                      3372               3372               same           
  Task Computation Energy (J)      2529000.0000       610720.0000        ↓ 75.9%
  Total Delay (ms)                 16897.6339         3206.2800          ↓ 81.0%
  Energy per Task (J)              750.0000           181.1151           avg per task
  Delay per Task (ms)              5.0112             0.9509             avg per task
  Tasks → EDGE                     0 (all cloud)      3364               ✓ offloaded    
  Tasks → FOG                      0 (all cloud)      0                  -              
  Tasks → CLOUD                    3372               0                  -              
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  WHY MOAOA WINS:
  • Edge nodes process tasks at 0.4 J/MI vs cloud 1.5 J/MI (73% less energy)
  • Edge comm delay: dataSize/10000 vs cloud: dataSize/100 (100x faster)
  • 3364 tasks kept at edge, avoiding cloud round-trip overhead
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
